## Idea

A map `f : A → B` is **surjective** if all of its
[fibers](foundation-core.fibers-of-maps.md) are
[inhabited](foundation.inhabited-types.md).

## Definition

### Surjective maps

### The type of all surjective maps out of a type

### Any equivalence is surjective

### A map into a proposition is a propositional truncation if and only if it is surjective

<pre class="Agda"><a id="12837" class="Keyword">abstract</a>
  <a id="is-surjective-is-propositional-truncation"></a><a id="12848" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12848" class="Function">is-surjective-is-propositional-truncation</a> <a id="12890" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="12896" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12897" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12897" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="12900" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12900" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="12903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12905" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="12910" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12913" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12913" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12915" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12917" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="12920" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12897" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="12922" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12924" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12925" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12925" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="12927" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12929" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#949" class="Function">Prop</a> <a id="12934" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12900" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="12936" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12939" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12939" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12943" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12913" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12945" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12947" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1045" class="Function">type-Prop</a> <a id="12957" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12925" class="Bound">P</a><a id="12958" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12960" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="12966" href="foundation.universal-property-propositional-truncation.html#3048" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-propositional-truncation</a> <a id="13020" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12925" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="13022" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12939" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13024" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="13030" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#2240" class="Function">is-surjective</a> <a id="13044" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#12939" class="Bound">f</a>

### Functoriality of products preserves being surjective

<pre class="Agda"><a id="14987" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14994" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#14994" class="Module">_</a>

### If a composite is surjective, then so is its left factor

<pre class="Agda"><a id="16483" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="16490" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16490" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="16494" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16495" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16495" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="16498" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16498" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="16501" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16501" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="16504" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16506" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="16511" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16513" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16514" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16514" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16516" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16518" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16521" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16495" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="16523" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16525" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16526" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16526" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="16528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16530" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16533" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16498" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="16535" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16537" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16538" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16538" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16540" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16542" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16545" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16501" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="16547" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="16551" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="16560" class="Keyword">abstract</a>
    <a id="16573" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#16573" class="Function">is-surjective-right-map-triangle</a> <a id="16606" class="Symbol">:</a>

### Precomposing functions into a family of `k+1`-types by a surjective map is a `k`-truncated map

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-trunc-map-precomp-Π-is-surjective"></a><a id="18208" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18208" class="Function">is-trunc-map-precomp-Π-is-surjective</a> <a id="18245" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="18249" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18250" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18250" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="18253" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18253" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="18256" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18256" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="18259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18261" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="18266" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18268" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18269" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18269" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="18271" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18273" href="foundation-core.truncation-levels.html#521" class="Datatype">𝕋</a><a id="18274" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18276" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="18280" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18281" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18281" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18283" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18285" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="18288" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18250" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="18290" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18293" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18293" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18295" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18297" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="18300" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18253" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="18302" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18304" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18305" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18305" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18307" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18309" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18281" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18313" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18293" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18314" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18316" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18318" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#2240" class="Function">is-surjective</a> <a id="18332" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18305" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18334" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="18338" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18339" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18339" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="18341" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18343" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18293" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18345" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18347" href="foundation-core.truncated-types.html#1534" class="Function">Truncated-Type</a> <a id="18362" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18256" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="18365" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18366" href="foundation-core.truncation-levels.html#558" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-𝕋</a> <a id="18373" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#18269" class="Bound">k</a><a id="18374" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18377" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="22513" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22515" href="foundation-core.embeddings.html#1757" class="Function">equiv-ap-emb</a> <a id="22528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22529" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#3761" class="Function">emb-inclusion-Surjection-Into-Truncated-Type</a> <a id="22574" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#21872" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="22577" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#21885" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="22579" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#21893" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22580" class="Symbol">))</a>

### The type `Surjection-Into-Truncated-Type l2 (succ-𝕋 k) A` is `k`-truncated

This remains to be shown.
[#735](https://github.com/UniMath/agda-unimath/issues/735)

### Postcomposition of extensions along surjective maps by an embedding is an equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24966" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24973" href="foundation.surjective-maps.html#24973" class="Module">_</a>

### The type of surjections `A ↠ B` is equivalent to the type of families `P` of inhabited types over `B` equipped with an equivalence `A ≃ Σ B P`

This remains to be shown.
[#735](https://github.com/UniMath/agda-unimath/issues/735)

## See also

- In
  [Epimorphisms with respect to sets](foundation.epimorphisms-with-respect-to-sets.md)
  we show that a map is surjective if and only if it is an epimorphism with
  respect to sets.
